# Cup Racing League Index

Cup Racing is a private sim racing league running on iRacing and Assetto Corsa.
Odd-numbered seasons use formula cars; even-numbered seasons use sports/GT cars.
Season 18 was split into S18a and S18b (both sports car seasons).

## Season Registry

| Season | Type | Car | Venues | Races/Venue | WDC | WCC |

## Scoring System

Standard scoring (S2 onwards): Pole = 1pt bonus, Fastest Lap = 1pt bonus.
Season 1 exception: Pole = 2pts, Fastest Lap = 2pts.
Position points: P1=30, P2=25, P3=22, P4=20, P5=18, P6=16, P7=14, P8=13, P9=12, P10=11, P11=10, P12=9, P13=8, P14=7, P15=6, P16=5, P17=4, P18=3, P19=2, P20=1.

## Weighted Score Formula

Win% x 0.20 + Podium% x 0.20 + Top 5 Rate x 0.20 + Pts/Race x 0.20 + Points Rate x 0.10 + FL Rate x 0.05 + Pole Rate x 0.05

All component metrics are normalized so the best value in each category = 1.0.
The raw score is then multiplied by a penalty discount (2% per penalty, floor 85%)
and a field size factor (proportional to league average grid size, floor 80%).

# Cup Racing Career Statistics

Cumulative career statistics for all drivers across all completed seasons.

## Championship Winners

- **Josie**: 17 WDC, 12 WCC
- **James**: 3 WDC, 4 WCC
- **Toby**: 2 WDC, 10 WCC
- **Lee**: 1 WDC, 6 WCC
- **Green Kyle**: 1 WDC, 2 WCC

## Driver Career Summaries

### Josie — Career Summary
Josie has competed in 328 races across Cup Racing history. 17x World Drivers' Champion. 12x World Constructors' Champion. 160 wins (48.8% win rate). 261 podiums (79.6% podium rate). 237 pole positions. 218 fastest laps (66.5% FL rate). 8767 career points (26.7 pts/race). 299 top-5 finishes (91.2% top-5 rate).

### James — Career Summary
James has competed in 312 races across Cup Racing history. 3x World Drivers' Champion. 4x World Constructors' Champion. 68 wins (21.8% win rate). 206 podiums (66.0% podium rate). 69 pole positions. 82 fastest laps (26.3% FL rate). 7135 career points (22.9 pts/race). 268 top-5 finishes (85.9% top-5 rate).

### Lee — Career Summary
Lee has competed in 274 races across Cup Racing history. 1x World Drivers' Champion. 6x World Constructors' Champion. 32 wins (11.7% win rate). 134 podiums (48.9% podium rate). 17 pole positions. 17 fastest laps (6.2% FL rate). 5558 career points (20.3 pts/race). 201 top-5 finishes (73.4% top-5 rate).

### Brie — Career Summary
Brie has competed in 241 races across Cup Racing history. 1x World Constructors' Champion. 11 wins (4.6% win rate). 77 podiums (32.0% podium rate). 6 fastest laps (2.5% FL rate). 4495 career points (18.7 pts/race). 163 top-5 finishes (67.6% top-5 rate).

### Toby — Career Summary
Toby has competed in 209 races across Cup Racing history. 2x World Drivers' Champion. 10x World Constructors' Champion. 31 wins (14.8% win rate). 102 podiums (48.8% podium rate). 22 pole positions. 24 fastest laps (11.5% FL rate). 4335 career points (20.7 pts/race). 161 top-5 finishes (77.0% top-5 rate).

### Colin — Career Summary

# Cup Racing Career Performance Index (CPI)

The CPI is a composite metric measuring overall career quality, combining:
average weighted score, peak weighted score, average points rate, average top-5 rate, WDCs, and WCCs.

# Cup Racing Weighted Score Rankings (WSR)

Weighted scores rank individual driver-season performances using raw stats:
Win% (0.20) + Podium% (0.20) + Top 5 Rate (0.20) + Pts/Race (0.20) + Points Rate (0.10) + FL Rate (0.05) + Pole Rate (0.05)

Scores are normalized so the best performance in each category = 1.0.
The raw score is then adjusted by two multipliers:
- **Penalty discount**: each penalty costs 2% of the score (floor: 85%).
- **Field size**: seasons with smaller fields are discounted proportionally against the league average (floor: 80%).

# Cup Racing Career Rating

The Career Rating tracks each driver's form across seasons using an Elo-style system
built on Bayesian-smoothed per-season metrics. Every driver starts at 1000. Each season,
the rating moves based on performance relative to a bracket-aware expected score:

- **Soft brackets**: each driver's expected score is the Gaussian-weighted average of
  nearby-rated drivers' season scores. No hard brackets — the comparison group blends
  smoothly based on rating proximity (sigma = 200 rating points). When a driver has
  fewer than 4 effective Gaussian peers, the expected score blends toward the average
  of the 4 nearest drivers by rating — so outlier drivers are always measured against
  their closest rivals, not the whole field.
- **K-factor**: controls responsiveness. Starts at 0.80 for debut seasons, decays with
  career length but never drops below 0.40 — veterans always respond to recent form.
- **Confidence**: rating changes scale with participation (races driven ÷ season total,
  floor: 50%). More races = more certainty in the result.
- **Upset bonus**: drivers earn extra rating for outscoring higher-rated opponents with
  similar participation. One-directional — no penalty for losing to lower-rated drivers.
- **Weights**: Win% (0.18), Podium% (0.17), Top 5 Rate (0.20), Pts/Race (0.20),
  FL Rate (0.10), Pole Rate (0.05), Points Rate (0.10).

Per-season inputs are Bayesian-smoothed with field-adjusted priors — small sample seasons
(few races) are pulled toward what we'd expect from a random driver in that field size,
preventing fluky short appearances from distorting ratings.
